Document Purpose / à¦¡à¦•à§à¦®à§‡à¦¨à§à¦Ÿà§‡à¦° à¦‰à¦¦à§à¦¦à§‡à¦¶à§à¦¯
This Software Requirements Specification (SRS) document describes the functional and non-functional requirements for the â€œEmployee Productivity &amp; Computer Monitoring SaaS Platformâ€, designed primarily for the Bangladesh corporate market. It is intended for use by the development team, project stakeholders, QA engineers, and business analysts as the single source of truth for system scope and behavior.
à¦à¦‡ SRS à¦¡à¦•à§à¦®à§‡à¦¨à§à¦Ÿà¦Ÿà¦¿ â€œà¦à¦®à¦ªà§à¦²à¦¯à¦¼à¦¿ à¦ªà§à¦°à§‹à¦¡à¦¾à¦•à§à¦Ÿà¦¿à¦­à¦¿à¦Ÿà¦¿ à¦“ à¦•à¦®à§à¦ªà¦¿à¦‰à¦Ÿà¦¾à¦° à¦®à¦¨à¦¿à¦Ÿà¦°à¦¿à¦‚ SaaS à¦ªà§à¦²à§à¦¯à¦¾à¦Ÿà¦«à¦°à§à¦®â€-à¦à¦° à¦•à¦¾à¦°à§à¦¯à¦•à¦°à§€ (Functional) à¦à¦¬à¦‚ à¦…-à¦•à¦¾à¦°à§à¦¯à¦•à¦°à§€ (Non-Functional) à¦šà¦¾à¦¹à¦¿à¦¦à¦¾ à¦¬à¦°à§à¦£à¦¨à¦¾ à¦•à¦°à§‡, à¦¯à¦¾ à¦®à§‚à¦²à¦¤ à¦¬à¦¾à¦‚à¦²à¦¾à¦¦à§‡à¦¶à§‡à¦° à¦•à¦°à§à¦ªà§‹à¦°à§‡à¦Ÿ à¦®à¦¾à¦°à§à¦•à§‡à¦Ÿà§‡à¦° à¦œà¦¨à§à¦¯ à¦¡à¦¿à¦œà¦¾à¦‡à¦¨ à¦•à¦°à¦¾ à¦¹à¦šà§à¦›à§‡à¥¤ à¦à¦‡ à¦¡à¦•à§à¦®à§‡à¦¨à§à¦Ÿ à¦¡à§‡à¦­à§‡à¦²à¦ªà¦®à§‡à¦¨à§à¦Ÿ à¦Ÿà¦¿à¦®, à¦¸à§à¦Ÿà§‡à¦•à¦¹à§‹à¦²à§à¦¡à¦¾à¦°, QA à¦‡à¦žà§à¦œà¦¿à¦¨à¦¿à¦¯à¦¼à¦¾à¦° à¦à¦¬à¦‚ à¦¬à¦¿à¦œà¦¨à§‡à¦¸ à¦…à§à¦¯à¦¾à¦¨à¦¾à¦²à¦¿à¦¸à§à¦Ÿà¦¦à§‡à¦° à¦œà¦¨à§à¦¯ à¦¸à¦¿à¦¸à§à¦Ÿà§‡à¦®à§‡à¦° à¦¸à§à¦¯à§‹à¦— à¦“ à¦†à¦šà¦°à¦£ à¦¸à¦‚à¦•à§à¦°à¦¾à¦¨à§à¦¤ à¦à¦•à¦• à¦°à§‡à¦«à¦¾à¦°à§‡à¦¨à§à¦¸ à¦¹à¦¿à¦¸à§‡à¦¬à§‡ à¦¬à§à¦¯à¦¬à¦¹à§ƒà¦¤ à¦¹à¦¬à§‡à¥¤
1. Introduction / à¦­à§‚à¦®à¦¿à¦•à¦¾
1.1 Purpose / à¦‰à¦¦à§à¦¦à§‡à¦¶à§à¦¯
The purpose of this project is to design and develop an Enterprise-Grade, Multi-Tenant SaaS platform that enables organizations operating in Bangladesh to monitor employee computer activity, measure productivity, and generate actionable analytics and reports for HR and management decision-making.
à¦à¦‡ à¦ªà§à¦°à¦œà§‡à¦•à§à¦Ÿà§‡à¦° à¦‰à¦¦à§à¦¦à§‡à¦¶à§à¦¯ à¦¹à¦²à§‹ à¦à¦•à¦Ÿà¦¿ à¦à¦¨à§à¦Ÿà¦¾à¦°à¦ªà§à¦°à¦¾à¦‡à¦œ-à¦—à§à¦°à§‡à¦¡, à¦®à¦¾à¦²à§à¦Ÿà¦¿-à¦Ÿà§‡à¦¨à§à¦¯à¦¾à¦¨à§à¦Ÿ SaaS à¦ªà§à¦²à§à¦¯à¦¾à¦Ÿà¦«à¦°à§à¦® à¦¤à§ˆà¦°à¦¿ à¦•à¦°à¦¾, à¦¯à¦¾à¦° à¦®à¦¾à¦§à§à¦¯à¦®à§‡ à¦¬à¦¾à¦‚à¦²à¦¾à¦¦à§‡à¦¶à§‡ à¦ªà¦°à¦¿à¦šà¦¾à¦²à¦¿à¦¤ à¦ªà§à¦°à¦¤à¦¿à¦·à§à¦ à¦¾à¦¨à¦¸à¦®à§‚à¦¹ à¦¤à¦¾à¦¦à§‡à¦° à¦•à¦°à§à¦®à§€à¦¦à§‡à¦° à¦•à¦®à§à¦ªà¦¿à¦‰à¦Ÿà¦¾à¦° à¦•à¦¾à¦°à§à¦¯à¦•à§à¦°à¦® à¦®à¦¨à¦¿à¦Ÿà¦° à¦•à¦°à¦¤à§‡ à¦ªà¦¾à¦°à¦¬à§‡, à¦ªà§à¦°à§‹à¦¡à¦¾à¦•à§à¦Ÿà¦¿à¦­à¦¿à¦Ÿà¦¿ à¦ªà¦°à¦¿à¦®à¦¾à¦ª à¦•à¦°à¦¤à§‡ à¦ªà¦¾à¦°à¦¬à§‡ à¦à¦¬à¦‚ HR à¦“ à¦®à§à¦¯à¦¾à¦¨à§‡à¦œà¦®à§‡à¦¨à§à¦Ÿà§‡à¦° à¦¸à¦¿à¦¦à§à¦§à¦¾à¦¨à§à¦¤ à¦—à§à¦°à¦¹à¦£à§‡à¦° à¦œà¦¨à§à¦¯ à¦•à¦¾à¦°à§à¦¯à¦•à¦° à¦…à§à¦¯à¦¾à¦¨à¦¾à¦²à¦¿à¦Ÿà¦¿à¦•à§à¦¸ à¦“ à¦°à¦¿à¦ªà§‹à¦°à§à¦Ÿ à¦¤à§ˆà¦°à¦¿ à¦•à¦°à¦¤à§‡ à¦ªà¦¾à¦°à¦¬à§‡à¥¤
1.2 Scope / à¦¸à§à¦¯à§‹à¦—
The system consists of three major components:
A central Web-based SaaS Platform (Backend API + React Admin Dashboard) supporting multiple companies (tenants) with isolated data.
A lightweight Desktop Monitoring Agent (Windows-first, with macOS roadmap) installed on employee computers, which collects activity data and synchronizes with the central platform.
A reporting &amp; analytics engine that converts raw activity data into productivity scores, dashboards, and exportable reports.

1.5 Bangladesh Market Context / à¦¬à¦¾à¦‚à¦²à¦¾à¦¦à§‡à¦¶ à¦®à¦¾à¦°à§à¦•à§‡à¦Ÿ à¦ªà§à¦°à§‡à¦•à§à¦·à¦¾à¦ªà¦Ÿ
This platform is being designed specifically for deployment to companies operating within Bangladesh. This drives several requirements that differ from a generic global SaaS product, including local payment gateway integration, Bengali language support, data residency considerations, on-premise deployment options, and compliance with local labour and data protection norms.

2. Overall Description / à¦¸à¦¾à¦®à¦—à§à¦°à¦¿à¦• à¦¬à¦°à§à¦£à¦¨à¦¾
2.1 Product Perspective / à¦ªà§à¦°à§‹à¦¡à¦¾à¦•à§à¦Ÿ à¦ªà¦¾à¦°à§à¦¸à¦ªà§‡à¦•à§à¦Ÿà¦¿à¦­
The platform is a new, standalone, multi-tenant SaaS product. It is composed of a Laravel-based backend API, a React-based web dashboard, a C# desktop monitoring agent, and supporting infrastructure (PostgreSQL, Redis, object storage).

7. Development Roadmap / à¦¡à§‡à¦­à§‡à¦²à¦ªà¦®à§‡à¦¨à§à¦Ÿ à¦°à§‹à¦¡à¦®à§à¦¯à¦¾à¦ª
Given the scope of an enterprise SaaS platform, development is organized into four phases to ensure faster time-to-market and iterative feedback.
à¦à¦¨à§à¦Ÿà¦¾à¦°à¦ªà§à¦°à¦¾à¦‡à¦œ SaaS à¦ªà§à¦²à§à¦¯à¦¾à¦Ÿà¦«à¦°à§à¦®à§‡à¦° à¦¬à§à¦¯à¦¾à¦ªà§à¦¤à¦¿ à¦¬à¦¿à¦¬à§‡à¦šà¦¨à¦¾à¦¯à¦¼, à¦¦à§à¦°à§à¦¤ à¦®à¦¾à¦°à§à¦•à§‡à¦Ÿà§‡ à¦†à¦¨à¦¾à¦° à¦œà¦¨à§à¦¯ à¦¡à§‡à¦­à§‡à¦²à¦ªà¦®à§‡à¦¨à§à¦Ÿ à¦šà¦¾à¦°à¦Ÿà¦¿ à¦«à§‡à¦œà§‡ à¦¬à¦¿à¦­à¦•à§à¦¤ à¦•à¦°à¦¾ à¦¹à¦¯à¦¼à§‡à¦›à§‡à¥¤
Phase 1 â€” MVP (Core Foundation)
Auth, RBAC, multi-tenant base setup
Windows Agent: app/website tracking, idle detection, screenshots
Basic web dashboard with company/device/employee management
Local payment gateway integration (SSLCommerz/bKash) for subscriptions
Phase 2 â€” Analytics &amp; Real-Time
Productivity scoring engine, daily/weekly/monthly reports
Real-time dashboard via WebSocket
PDF/Excel/CSV export
Consent &amp; data retention module
Phase 3 â€” Enterprise Expansion
macOS agent
SSO (Google Workspace / Azure AD) for enterprise clients
On-premise deployment package
Advanced department/team analytics
Phase 4 â€” Advanced / Future
AI-based anomaly detection in work patterns
Mobile device monitoring (optional)
White-label/reseller support
